FROM (
    SELECT c.request_id, c.complaint_id, c.created_at, c.remarks, c.request_status_id, c.request_type_id, c.requested_by, c.reviewed_at, c.reviewed_by
    FROM complaint_requests AS c
    WHERE c.requested_by = @requestedBy_Value AND c.request_type_id = @requestTypeId_Value
    ORDER BY c.created_at DESC
    LIMIT @p3 OFFSET @p
) AS c1
INNER JOIN complaints AS c0 ON c1.complaint_id = c0.complaint_id
INNER JOIN request_types AS r ON c1.request_type_id = r.request_type_id
INNER JOIN request_statuses AS r0 ON c1.request_status_id = r0.request_status_id
INNER JOIN employees AS e ON c1.requested_by = e.employee_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e0 ON c1.reviewed_by = e0.employee_id
ORDER BY c1.created_at DESC

SELECT c.complaint_id, c.category_id, c.closed_at, c.complaint_description, c.complaint_title, c.created_at, c.current_handler_employee_id, c.escalation_due_at, c.escalation_level, c.priority_id, c.raised_by_employee_id, c.reopened_count, c.resolved_at, c.status_id, c.updated_at, c0.category_id, c0.category_name, c0.created_at, c0.default_priority_id, c0.department_id, c0.is_active, c0.sla_hours, c0.updated_at, p.priority_id, p.escalation_order, p.priority_name, e.employee_id, e.created_at, e.department_id, e.email, e.employee_name, e.is_active, e.mobile_number, e.password_hash, e.role_id, e.updated_at
FROM complaints AS c
INNER JOIN categories AS c0 ON c.category_id = c0.category_id
INNER JOIN priorities AS p ON c.priority_id = p.priority_id
LEFT JOIN employees AS e ON c.current_handler_employee_id = e.employee_id
WHERE c.escalation_due_at <= now() AND c.status_id <> 6 AND c.status_id <> 7 AND c.status_id <> 9 AND c.status_id <> 5
